# 2026-02-11 · quant-ph 论文速递


## 集成人工智能和量子启发技术实现高效酶发酵优化

**Original Title:** Integrating AI and Quantum-Inspired Techniques for Efficient Enzyme Fermentation Optimization

**Authors:** Ying-Wei Tseng, Yu-Ting Kao, Yeong-Jar Chang, Jia-Han Ou, Wen-Zhi Zhang, Jin-Jia Wang, Yung-Hsiang Lin

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.06420v2

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.06420v2

**Submitted:** 2026-02-06


### 摘要

本文介绍了一种将人工智能（AI）和量子启发技术相结合的新方法，以提高多变量优化实验的效率。与传统物理实验相比，通过使用先进的软件模拟，这种方法显着减少了时间和成本。该研究重点关注酶发酵，证明这种方法可以用更少的实验取得更好的结果。研究结果凸显了这种方法更有效地识别最佳配方的潜力，从而推动酶发酵和其他需要复杂优化的领域的进步。最初，即使经过600次实验，活性成分（AIN）也无法得到改进。然而，通过采用本文概述的方法，我们仅在405次实验中就找到了更好的配方。这导致AIN从8481增加到10068，提高了18.7%。


### Abstract

This paper introduces a new method that combines Artificial Intelligence (AI) and quantum-inspired techniques to improve the efficiency of multi-variable optimization experiments. By using advanced software simulations, this approach significantly reduces the time and cost compared to traditional physical experiments. The research focuses on enzyme fermentation, demonstrating that this method can achieve better results with fewer experiments. The findings highlight the potential of this approach to more effectively identify optimal formulations, leading to advancements in enzyme fermentation and other fields that require complex optimization. Initially, the Active Ingredients (AIN) could not be improved even after 600 experiments. However, by adopting the method outlined in this paper, we were able to identify a better formula in just 405 experiments. This resulted in an increase of AIN from 8481 to 10068, representing an improvement of 18.7%.


---


## 基于Markov的非Hermitian多体定位诊断的局限性

**Original Title:** Limitations of SVD-Based Diagnostics for Non-Hermitian Many-Body Localization with Time-Reversal Symmetry

**Authors:** Huimin You, Jinghu Liu, Yunbo Zhang, Zhihao Xu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07349v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07349v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

奇异值分解（DID）已被用来为非Hermitian多体系统构建类似Hermitian的诊断，但其识别多体定位（MBL）转变的可靠性--特别是在时间反转对称（TRS）保留设置中--仍然不清楚。在这里，我们根据具有非互惠跳跃的TRS保留非厄米特硬核玻色子链中的精确对角化（ED）来对基于VD的诊断进行基准测试，并考虑三个代表性势：准周期势、随机无序和斯塔克势。我们比较了谱统计数据、半链纠缠量、逆参与比和谱形状因子。对于准周期和随机无序模型，ED产生相互一致的转变估计，而奇异值系统地将推断的临界无序强度转移到更大的值，并可能导致不同的阶段分配。相比之下，对于干净的斯塔克模型，ED和奇异值定位一致的临界倾斜。我们的结果表明，虽然基于VD的诊断捕捉了定性趋势，但它们对于定量定位保留TRS的非Hermitian多体系统中的MBL转变通常并不可靠。


### Abstract

Singular value decomposition (SVD) has been used to construct Hermitian-like diagnostics for non-Hermitian many-body systems, but its reliability for identifying many-body localization (MBL) transitions -- particularly in time-reversal-symmetry (TRS) preserving settings -- remains unclear. Here we benchmark SVD-based diagnostics against exact diagonalization (ED) in TRS-preserving non-Hermitian hard-core-boson chains with nonreciprocal hopping, considering three representative potentials: a quasiperiodic potential, random disorder, and a Stark potential. We compare spectral statistics, half-chain entanglement entropy, inverse participation ratio, and spectral form factors. For the quasiperiodic and random-disorder models, ED yields mutually consistent transition estimates, whereas SVD systematically shifts the inferred critical disorder strength to larger values and can lead to different phase assignments. In contrast, for the clean Stark model ED and SVD locate a consistent critical tilt. Our results show that while SVD-based diagnostics capture qualitative trends, they are not generically reliable for quantitatively locating the MBL transition in TRS-preserving non-Hermitian many-body systems.


---


## 编码很重要：量子组合优化的二进制和D元表示基准

**Original Title:** Encoding Matters: Benchmarking Binary and D-ary Representations for Quantum Combinatorial Optimization

**Authors:** Shashank Sanjay Bhat, Peiyong Wang, Joseph West, Udaya Parampalli

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07357v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07357v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

组合优化问题通常使用二次无约束二元优化（QUBO）来制定，其中通过引入辅助变量并迅速增加汉密尔顿复杂性的惩罚项来实施约束，从而限制了近期量子设备的可扩展性。在这项工作中，我们系统地研究了二次无约束D元优化（QUDO）作为一种替代公式，其中决策变量直接编码在更高维度的希尔伯特空间中。我们证明，QUDO自然地捕捉了一系列问题类别的结构约束，包括旅行推销员问题、车辆路径问题的两个变体、图着色、作业调度和Max-K-Cut，而不需要大量的罚结构。使用量子逼近优化算法（qudit QAOA）的qudit级实现，我们将这些公式与其二进制QUBO对应物和精确经典解进行基准测试。我们的研究表明，在相当的电路深度下，逼近比持续提高，计算负担大幅减少，突出表明QUDO是量子组合优化的可扩展和表达性表示。


### Abstract

Combinatorial optimization problems are typically formulated using Quadratic Unconstrained Binary Optimization (QUBO), where constraints are enforced through penalty terms that introduce auxiliary variables and rapidly increase Hamiltonian complexity, limiting scalability on near term quantum devices. In this work, we systematically study Quadratic Unconstrained D-ary Optimization (QUDO) as an alternative formulation in which decision variables are encoded directly in higher dimensional Hilbert spaces. We demonstrate that QUDO naturally captures structural constraints across a range of problem classes, including the Traveling Salesman Problem, two variants of the Vehicle Routing Problem, graph coloring, job scheduling, and Max-K-Cut, without the need for extensive penalty constructions. Using a qudit-level implementation of the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (qudit QAOA), we benchmark these formulations against their binary QUBO counterparts and exact classical solutions. Our study show consistently improved approximation ratios and substantially reduced computational overhead at comparable circuit depths, highlighting QUDO as a scalable and expressive representation for quantum combinatorial optimization.


---


## 里德伯原子多体系统中的非厄米特物理学

**Original Title:** Non-Hermitian physics in the many-body system of Rydberg atoms

**Authors:** Ya-Jun Wang, Jun Zhang, Dong-Sheng Ding

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07372v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07372v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

非埃尔米特物理学表现出超越传统埃尔米特系统的独特物理性质，例如对称性破缺、异常点的出现、拓扑相转变等。这些现象已在各个平台上得到了广泛研究，包括量子光学、冷原子系统、超导电路和凝聚物质物理学。里德伯原子具有远程相互作用和灵活的可控性，为非埃尔米特物理学的实验实现提供了一个有前途的平台。本文主要总结了近年来莱德堡原子体系非厄米特物理学领域取得的关键实验和理论成果。它概述了非厄米哈密顿量的基本结构，揭示了里德伯原子相互作用引起的有效耗散机制，并讨论了它们对光谱特性和对称性破缺的影响。这些研究不仅加深了对非厄米多体系统量子相变的理解，而且突出了Rydberg原子平台在实现和控制拓扑态方面的独特价值。


### Abstract

Non-Hermitian physics exhibits unique physical properties beyond those of traditional Hermitian systems, such as symmetry breaking, the emergence of exceptional points, topological phase transitions, and more. These phenomena have been extensively studied across various platforms, including quantum optics, cold atom systems, superconducting circuits, and condensed matter physics. Rydberg atoms, with their long-range interactions and flexible controllability, provide a promising platform for the experimental realization of non-Hermitian physics. This review primarily summarizes the key experimental and theoretical achievements in the field of non-Hermitian physics within Rydberg atomic systems in recent years. It outlines the fundamental construction of non-Hermitian Hamiltonians, reveals the effective dissipation mechanisms induced by Rydberg atomic interactions, and discusses their impact on spectral properties and symmetry breaking. These studies not only deepen the understanding of quantum phase transitions in non-Hermitian many-body systems but also highlight the unique value of Rydberg atomic platforms in realizing and controlling topological states.


---


## ABL规则和后选择的危险

**Original Title:** The ABL Rule and the Perils of Post-Selection

**Authors:** Jacob A. Barandes

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07402v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07402v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

1964年，阿哈罗诺夫、伯格曼和莱博维茨引入了他们著名的ABL规则，旨在为计算量子理论中的新型条件概率提供一种时间对称的形式体系。后来的论文赋予ABL规则额外的重要性，包括断言它支持违反不确定性原则。目前的工作对这些主张以及随后挽救ABL规则原始解释的尝试提出了质疑。从更广泛的角度来看，本文指出了ABL规则核心的一个微妙的类别错误，该错误包括属于单个系统的可观察量与仅针对物理整体出现的可观察量的混淆。一路上，本文指出了围绕ABL规则的研究文献中的其他问题和谬误推理，包括后选择的滥用、对经典公式模式匹配的依赖以及将实验数据视为解释问题的答案的测量论立场。


### Abstract

In 1964, Aharonov, Bergmann, and Lebowitz introduced their well-known ABL rule with the intention of providing a time-symmetric formalism for computing novel kinds of conditional probabilities in quantum theory. Later papers attached additional significance to the ABL rule, including assertions that it supported violations of the uncertainty principle. The present work challenges these claims, as well as subsequent attempts to salvage the original interpretation of the ABL rule. Taking a broader view, this paper identifies a subtle category error at the heart of the ABL rule that consists of confusing observables that belong to a single system with emergent observables that arise only for physical ensembles. Along the way, this paper points out other problems and fallacious reasoning in the research literature surrounding the ABL rule, including the misuse of post-selection, a reliance on pattern matching to classical formulas, and a posture of measurementism that takes experimental data as providing answers to interpretational questions.


---


## 局域态集发光的量子多体原理

**Original Title:** Quantum Many-Body Principles of Localized-State Ensemble Luminescence

**Authors:** Xinye Fan, Shijie Xu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07406v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07406v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

由缺陷和杂质等各种无序引起的定域电子状态通常存在于固体中。它们的光学性质，特别是发光性质，具有科学和技术意义。但这种定域态系综（LSE）发光的微观理论尚未建立。在这封信中，我们试图通过发展考虑电子-音素（e-p）和电子-电子（e-e）相互作用的量子多体（MB）发光理论来填补这个空白。通过使用发展的MB-LSE理论，峰位红移和随后的蓝移、谱宽变窄和随后的增宽、强度下降和寿命变化等异常热行为可以被定量解释，从而阐明了电子-音素和电子-电子相互作用在可变温度LSE发光中的作用。此外，在MB-LSE理论的框架内，进一步推导并讨论了Varshni的带隙温度依赖性经验公式和e-p耦合的Huang-Rhys因子。


### Abstract

Localized electron states induced by various disorders,including defects and impurities,usually exist in solids.Their optical properties,especially their luminescence properties,are of both scientific and technological significance.But a microscopic theory has not yet been established for such localized-state ensemble (LSE) luminescence.In this Letter,we attempt to fill this void via developing a quantum many-body (MB) luminescence theory taking into account both electron-phonon (e-p) and electron-electron (e-e) interactions.By using the developed MB-LSE theory,abnormal thermal behaviors such as redshift and subsequent blueshift of peak position,narrowing and succeeding broadening of linewidth,decline in intensity,and variation in lifetime can be quantitatively interpreted.The roles of electron-phonon and electron-electron interactions in the variable-temperature LSE luminescence are thus elucidated. Within the framework of the MB-LSE theory, moreover, Varshni's empirical formula for bandgap temperature dependence and Huang-Rhys factor for e-p coupling are further derived and discussed.


---


## 非Markovian穿着经过修饰的量子比特，具有局部退相

**Original Title:** Non-Markovianity in a dressed qubit with local dephasing

**Authors:** Saima Bashir, Muzaffar Qadir Lone, Prince A Ganai

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07438v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07438v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

我们研究了由两个晶格点之间的无自旋费米子跳跃实现的修饰量子比特的动力学，每个晶格点都与声子池强耦合。我们采用Lang-Firsov变换使问题易于处理的微扰。应用极化子框架下的无时间卷积主方程，我们研究了系统单重态-三重态基中修饰量子比特在宽范围的浴谱密度下的退相干动力学。它示出的相干性持续较长的时间尺度为大的耦合值，并显示非单调的行为，反映存在的非马尔可夫动力学。以一致性复兴和非单调衰变模式为特征的非马尔科夫性根据浴谱和耦合强度明显出现。与亚欧浴相结合的系统，无论是两者结合还是与另一种类型结合，在相对较小的耦合值下都显示出明显的记忆效应。相比之下，涉及Ohmic和超Ohmic浴的组合仅在较高的耦合下表现出明显的非马尔科夫性。


### Abstract

We study the dynamics of a dressed qubit implemented by a spinless fermion hopping between two lattice sites with each site strongly coupled to a bath of phonons. We employ Lang-Firsov transformation to make the problem tractable perturbatively. Applying time-convolutionless master equation within the polaron frame, we investigate decoherence dynamics of the dressed qubit within the singlet-triplet basis of the system for a wide range of bath spectral densities. It is shown that the coherence persists for longer time scales for large coupling values and shows non-monotonic behaviour reflecting the presence of non-Markovianity in the dynamics. Non-Markovianity, characterized by coherence revivals and non-monotonic decay patterns, emerges distinctly depending on the bath spectrum and coupling strengths. Systems coupled to sub-Ohmic baths, whether both or in combination with another type, display pronounced memory effects at relatively small values of couplings. In contrast, combinations involving Ohmic and super-Ohmic baths exhibit noticeable non-Markovianity only at higher couplings.


---


## TC/TLC和NETFD信息回流对应原理：结构单调性定理和最小相图

**Original Title:** TC/TCL and NETFD Correspondence Principles for Information Backflow: A Structural Monotonicity Theorem and Minimal Phase Diagrams

**Authors:** Koichi Nakagawa

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.09054v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.09054v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

我们为最小非马尔科夫松弛过程中的信息回流提出了一个统一的结构框架。中心思想是将非马尔科夫性解释为一种嵌入现象，其中可观察到的自由度与隐藏的辅助部门交换信息。我们的方法基于非平衡物理学中的两种标准形式：（i）时间卷积（TC）和无时间卷积（TLC）投影操作主方程，以及（ii）非平衡热场动力学（NETFD）的对应原理，它提供了相当于将密度操作员动力学嵌入到扩大空间中的载体演变中的双倍结构。我们定义了一个与信息量I（t）相关的一般信息回流函数N_I，并根据瞬时TLC生成元的整除性推导出不存在回流（N_I = 0）的充分条件。我们进一步将回流分解为经典和固有热场纠缠贡献，从而以与模型无关的方式对瞬时过冲和复兴现象进行分类。最小经典和量子双态模型作为分析上易于处理的例子进行了讨论，将Mittag-Leffler分数松弛恢复为普适信封。我们还提供了一种建设性的TC到TLC算法，用于提取有效速率并生成回流的相图。


### Abstract

We propose a unified structural framework for information backflow in minimal non-Markovian relaxation processes. The central idea is to interpret non-Markovianity as an embedding phenomenon in which observable degrees of freedom exchange information with hidden auxiliary sectors. Our approach is based on two standard formalisms in nonequilibrium physics: (i) the time-convolution (TC) and time-convolutionless (TCL) projection-operator master equations, and (ii) the correspondence principle of non-equilibrium thermo field dynamics (NETFD), which provides a doubling construction equivalent to an embedding of density-operator dynamics into a vector evolution in an enlarged space. We define a general information-backflow functional N_I associated with an information quantity I(t) and derive sufficient conditions for the absence of backflow (N_I = 0) in terms of divisibility properties of the instantaneous TCL generator. We further introduce a decomposition of backflow into classical and intrinsic thermo-field entanglement contributions, leading to a classification of transient overshoot and revival phenomena in a model-independent manner. Minimal classical and quantum two-state models are discussed as analytically tractable examples, recovering Mittag-Leffler fractional relaxation as a universal envelope. We also provide a constructive TC-to-TCL algorithm for extracting effective rates and producing phase diagrams of backflow.


---


## 用被动-主动反PT对称系统感知弱非调和性

**Original Title:** Sensing weak anharmonicities with a passive-active anti-PT symmetric system

**Authors:** Ya-Wei Zeng, Wei-Xin Chen, Tian-Le Yang, Wan-Jun Su, Huaizhi Wu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07460v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07460v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

我们提出了一种基于三模反宇称时间（反PT）对称腔-磁振子-导管系统的弱非调和性增强感知的方案。通过将光放大到有效腔模，即使两个消耗磁子模经历强的本征衰变，也可以灵活控制反PT对称Hamilton的谱宽抑制点。这一基本特征用于检测腔模和磁振子模中的弱非线性，两者都表现出相似的高灵敏度。此外，通过失调激光驱动可以大大提高灵敏度。基于集成无源-有源三模反PT对称系统，传感方案可以推广到各种具有非谐性的物理系统。


### Abstract

We propose a scheme for enhanced sensing of weak anharmonicities based on a three-mode anti-parity-time (anti-PT) symmetric cavity-magnon-waveguide system. By tuning the optical gain to the active cavity mode, the linewidth suppression point for the anti-PT symmetric Hamiltonian can be flexibly controlled even when the two dissipative magnonic modes experience strong intrinsic decay. This essential characteristic is utilized for detecting weak nonlinearities in both the cavity and magnonic modes, with both demonstrating similar high levels of sensitivity. Moreover, the sensitivity can be greatly improved with a detuned laser drive. Based on the integrated passive-active three-mode anti-PT symmetric system, the sensing scheme can be generalized to various physical systems with anharmonicities.


---


## 无线网络中干扰感知资源分配的递进QAOA

**Original Title:** Recursive QAOA for Interference-Aware Resource Allocation in Wireless Networks

**Authors:** Kuan-Cheng Chen, Hiromichi Matsuyama, Wei-hao Huang, Yu Yamashiro

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07483v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07483v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

密集无线网络中的离散无线资源管理问题自然被视为二次无约束二元优化（QUBO）程序，但很难大规模解决。我们研究了一种基于回归量子逼近优化算法（RQAOA）的量子经典方法，该方法通过测量的单量子位和双量子位相关器引导的变量消除来交织浅QAOA层。对于干扰感知的通道分配，我们给出了一个紧凑的QUBO/Ising公式，其中成对干扰会引起同通道耦合，并且通过二次罚分（或者，可选地，约束保持混合器）来实施一热约束。在RQAOA中，修复高置信度变量或关系可以减少问题维度、稳定训练，并将测量工作集中在缩小的实例上，一旦低于临界值，该实例就会得到解决。在中等大小的模拟实例上，包括四用户、四通道示例，该方法一致地返回可行的分配，并且对于演示的情况，获得全局最优值。这些结果表明，回归可以缓解影响普通QAOA的参数增长和可行性问题，并为无线资源分配中的近期量子试探法提出了一条可行的途径。


### Abstract

Discrete radio resource management problems in dense wireless networks are naturally cast as quadratic unconstrained binary optimization (QUBO) programs but are difficult to solve at scale. We investigate a quantum-classical approach based on the Recursive Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (RQAOA), which interleaves shallow QAOA layers with variable elimination guided by measured single- and two-qubit correlators. For interference-aware channel assignment, we give a compact QUBO/Ising formulation in which pairwise interference induces same-channel couplings and one-hot constraints are enforced via quadratic penalties (or, optionally, constraint-preserving mixers). Within RQAOA, fixing high-confidence variables or relations reduces the problem dimension, stabilizes training, and concentrates measurement effort on a shrinking instance that is solved exactly once below a cutoff. On simulated instances of modest size, including a four-user, four-channel example, the method consistently returns feasible assignments and, for the demonstrated case, attains the global optimum. These results indicate that recursion can mitigate parameter growth and feasibility issues that affect plain QAOA, and suggest a viable pathway for near-term quantum heuristics in wireless resource allocation.


---


## 无限维运算理论中Born型概率规则的因果刚性

**Original Title:** Causal Rigidity of Born-Type Probability Rules in Infinite-Dimensional Operational Theories

**Authors:** Enso O. Torres Alegre

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.09056v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.09056v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

我们为无限维设置中的广泛概率规则建立了操作刚性结果，适用于正态和转向假设。从广义概率理论的拓拓广出发，我们考虑定义为纯状态之间操作转移概率的函数的概率分配。我们表明，在三个操作驱动的要求下：没有超光速信号、通过西格玛加性意义上的纯化实现正常操纵的可用性以及在可计数的制备混合物下概率的西格玛亲和力，这一类中的任何可接受的规则都必须简化为同一性。特别是，非线性偏差通常会在转向场景中实现操作信号区分，而连续性与西格玛亲和力相结合则排除了非仿射替代方案。这确定了一个独特的因果不定点。在这类概率规则中，博恩规则成为唯一与承认正常操纵的操作理论中没有信号兼容的分配。我们通过冯诺伊曼代数的正常状态空间和GNS表示将运算结果与标准无限维量子力学联系起来，恢复了投影和广义测量的传统博恩规则。我们讨论了连续变量和量子场论体系中提出的后量子修改的假设范围和含义。


### Abstract

We establish an operational rigidity result for a broad class of probability rules in infinite-dimensional settings, applicable under normality and steering assumptions. Starting from a topological generalization of generalized probabilistic theories, we consider probability assignments defined as functions of an operational transition probability between pure states. We show that under three operationally motivated requirements: no superluminal signaling, availability of normal steering via purification in a sigma additive sense, and sigma affinity of probabilities under countable preparation mixtures, any admissible rule within this class must reduce to the identity. In particular, nonlinear deviations generically enable operational signaling distinctions in steering scenarios, while continuity combined with sigma affinity excludes non affine alternatives. This identifies a unique causal fixed point. Within this class of probability rules, the Born rule emerges as the only assignment compatible with no signaling in operational theories admitting normal steering. We connect the operational result to standard infinite-dimensional quantum mechanics through the normal state space of von Neumann algebras and the GNS representation, recovering the conventional Born rule for projective and generalized measurements. We discuss the scope of the assumptions and implications for proposed post quantum modifications in continuous variable and quantum field theoretic regimes.

## 热循环对量子位稳定性的系统化描述

**Original Title:** Systematic Characterization of Transmon Qubit Stability with Thermal Cycling

**Authors:** Cong Li, Zhaohua Yang, Xinfang Zhang, Zhihao Wu, Shichuan Xue, Mingtang Deng

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07522v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07522v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

量子位参数的时间稳定性和可重复性对于高温量子处理器的长期运行和维护至关重要。在这项工作中，我们对27个频率可调的转换子量子位进行了全面的纵向描述，该量子位跨越了一年多的四个热周期。我们的结果为高温硬件建立了一个独特的稳定性层次结构。我们发现，决定量子位频率和基线能量松弛时间（$T_1$）的固有设备参数对热应力表现出高度的鲁棒性，其特征在于频率偏差通常限制在0.5%内，并且不退化的相干基线。与此形成鲜明对比的是，环境变量，特别是背景磁通量补偿和两级系统（TL）缺陷的微观景观，在每个周期后都会经历显着的随机重新配置。通过采用频率相关的驰豫光谱和定量指标，$T_1$光谱Topography Fidelity，我们证明热循环可以作为局部缺陷环境的“硬重置”。该过程引入了相当于数千小时连续低温演变的光谱随机化水平。这些发现证实，虽然制造质量得到保留，但每个热循环的具体噪音实现在统计上是不同的，因此需要对大规模量子系统采取自动化重新校准策略。


### Abstract

The temporal stability and reproducibility of qubit parameters are critical for the long-term operation and maintenance of superconducting quantum processors. In this work, we present a comprehensive longitudinal characterization of 27 frequency-tunable transmon qubits spanning over one year across four thermal cycles. Our results establish a distinct hierarchy of stability for superconducting hardware. We find that the intrinsic device parameters determining the qubit frequency and the baseline energy relaxation times ($T_1$) exhibit high robustness against thermal stress, characterized by frequency deviations typically confined within 0.5\% and non-degraded coherence baselines. In stark contrast, the environmental variables, specifically the background magnetic flux offsets and the microscopic landscape of two-level system (TLS) defects, undergo a significant stochastic reconfiguration after each cycle. By employing frequency-dependent relaxation spectroscopy and a quantitative metric, the $T_1$ Spectral Topography Fidelity, we demonstrate that thermal cycling acts as a ``hard reset'' for the local defect environment. This process introduces a level of spectral randomization equivalent to thousands of hours of continuous low-temperature evolution. These findings confirm that while the fabrication quality is preserved, the specific noise realization is statistically distinct for each thermal cycle, necessitating automated recalibration strategies for large-scale quantum systems.

## 挤压增强双通道干涉用于低品质因子悬浮微磁铁的接地冷却

**Original Title:** Squeezing-enhanced dual-channel interference for ground-state cooling of a levitated micromagnet with low quality factor

**Authors:** Lei Chen, Zhe-qi Yang, Liang Bin, Zhi-Rong Zhong

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07531v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07531v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

将宏观振荡器的质量中心（CM）运动冷却到量子底态是在宏观尺度上测试量子力学的基本先决条件。然而，实现这一目标目前受到对NPS机械质量因子（$Q_c$）的严格要求的阻碍。在这里，我们提出了一种基于混合悬浮腔-磁机械系统中挤压增强量子干涉的双通道冷却方案，以克服这一限制。   通过协同磁振子CM和腔CM通道之间的压缩效应与量子干涉，我们的方案同时抑制斯托克斯（加热）散射，同时增强反斯托克斯（冷却）散射。~我们证明，这种冷却机制降低了三个数量级的基态冷却所需的临界$Q_c$，使其在实验上可达到的制度$Q_c \sim 10^4$。此外，与传统的单通道冷却相比，净冷却速率提高了近180倍。这种改善是伴随着两个数量级的减少，在稳态CM占用和冷却时间。重要的是，这种增强的性能即使在未分辨边带机制的深处也保持稳健。我们的结果为通过主动控制冷却动力学来制备宏观量子状态提供了一条可行的途径，从而放宽了对本征材料性质的限制。


### Abstract

Cooling the center-of-mass (CM) motion of a macroscopic oscillator to its quantum ground state is a fundamental prerequisite for testing quantum mechanics at macroscopic scales. However, achieving this goal is currently hindered by the stringent requirement for an ultrahigh mechanical quality factor ($Q_c$). Here, we propose a dual-channel cooling scheme based on squeezing-enhanced quantum interference within a hybrid levitated cavity-magnomechanical system to overcome this limitation.
  By synergizing squeezing effects with quantum interference between the magnon-CM and cavity-CM channels, our scheme simultaneously suppresses Stokes (heating) scattering while enhancing anti-Stokes (cooling) scattering.~We demonstrate that this cooling mechanism reduces the critical $Q_c$ required for ground-state cooling by three orders of magnitude, making it achievable in the experimentally accessible regime of $Q_c \sim 10^4$. Furthermore, the net cooling rate is enhanced by nearly 180-fold compared to that of conventional single-channel cooling. This improvement is accompanied by a two orders of magnitude reduction in both the steady-state CM occupancy and the cooling time. Importantly, this enhanced performance remains robust even deep within the unresolved-sideband regime. Our results provide a feasible path toward preparing macroscopic quantum states by actively controlling the cooling dynamics, thereby relaxing the constraints on intrinsic material properties.

## 基于NV的传感应用的光纤中自发荧光的特征

**Original Title:** Characterization of Autofluorescence in Optical Fibers for NV-based Sensing Applications

**Authors:** Stefan Johansson, Alexander Bukschat, Dennis Lönard, Alena Erlenbach, Jonas Gutsche, Artur Widera

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07536v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07536v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

光纤对于在各种传感应用中引导光至关重要。特别是对于量子传感器，如金刚石中的氮空位（NV）中心，它们可以实现光控制和器件小型化。然而，纤维内的荧光和散射（通常称为纤维背景、自发荧光或自发光）可以与NV中心的荧光在光谱上重叠，降低信噪比，从而限制传感器灵敏度。在这里，我们调查的标准光纤的光谱，考虑材料的依赖性，物理影响，以及它们的荧光定标与激发功率和波长。我们的结果以最少的不需要背景信号识别光谱成分和光纤类型，指导为基于NV的量子传感选择最佳光纤。


### Abstract

Optical fibers are crucial for guiding light in various sensing applications. Especially for quantum sensors such as the nitrogen-vacancy (NV) center in diamond, they enable light control and device miniaturization. However, fluorescence and scattering within the fiber, often referred to as fiber background, autofluorescence, or autoluminescence, can overlap spectrally with the NV centers' fluorescence, degrading the signal-to-noise ratio and thus limiting sensor sensitivity. Here, we investigate the optical spectra of standard optical fibers, considering material dependencies, physical influences, and their fluorescence scaling with excitation power and wavelength. Our results identify spectral components and fiber types with minimal unwanted background signals, guiding the selection of optimal fibers for NV-based quantum sensing.

## BiBiEQ：擦除量子位上的二元自行车代码

**Original Title:** BiBiEQ: Bivariate Bicycle Codes on Erasure Qubits

**Authors:** Ameya S. Bhave, Navnil Choudhury, Andrew Nemec, Kanad Basu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07578v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07578v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

擦除量子位通过将主要错误转换为称为擦除的可检测错误来减少容差量子错误纠正（QEC）的负担。他们在表面和Floquet代码存储器的阈值和扩展方面表现出了显着的改进。在这项工作中，我们对来自量子低密度Parity-check（QDLC）机制的二元自行车（BB）码使用擦除量子位。由于BB码的稀疏结构和有利的速率距离权衡，是QEC的实际候选者。我们引入BiBiEQ，这是一种新颖的框架，可以将给定的BB代码编译到擦除感知存储器电路C_E中。该擦除电路C_E包括在用户指定的擦除检查调度（2 EC、4 EC）上散布的擦除检查（EC）、重置和擦除。BiBiEQ将该擦除电路C_E转换为稳定器电路C，用于通用解码。BiBiEQ为此转换提供了两个引擎：BiBiBiEQ-Exact和BiBiEQ-Approx。BiBiEQ-Exact保留了联合擦除相关性，并作为我们的准确性基准，而BiBiBiEQ-Approx使用独立性逼近来加速大扫描并暴露准确性-吞吐量的权衡。使用BiBiEQ，我们对稳定器电路进行解码，以获得BB码的每轮逻辑错误率（LER），并量化EC调度对伪阈值以下的可纠正操作区域的影响。4 EC时间表使两种引擎的准确性保持接近，使BiBiEQ-Approx成为BiBiBiEQ-Exact的可靠代理，以实现更快的扫描。在伪阈值以下，码距离（d）从距离（d）6跳到10，BER下降幅度比距离（d）10到12大10- 17倍，表明大多数收益是在d=10时实现的。


### Abstract

Erasure qubits reduce overhead in fault-tolerant quantum error correction (QEC) by converting dominant faults into detectable errors known as erasures. They have demonstrated notable improvements in thresholds and scaling in surface and Floquet code memories. In this work, we use erasure qubits on Bivariate Bicycle (BB) codes from the quantum low-density parity-check (QLDPC) regime. Owing to their sparse structure and favorable rate-distance trade-offs, BB codes are practical candidates for QEC. We introduce BiBiEQ, a novel framework that compiles a given BB code into an erasure-aware memory circuit C_E. This erasure circuit C_E comprises erasure checks (ECs), resets, and erasures spread over a user-specified erasure check schedule (2EC, 4EC). BiBiEQ converts this erasure circuit C_E into the stabilizer circuit C for general-purpose decoding. BiBiEQ provides two engines for this conversion, BiBiEQ-Exact and BiBiEQ-Approx. BiBiEQ-Exact preserves the joint-erasure correlations and serves as our accuracy benchmark, while BiBiEQ-Approx uses an independence approximation to accelerate large sweeps and expose accuracy-throughput trade-offs. Using BiBiEQ, we decode the stabilizer circuits to get a per-round logical error rate (LER) for the BB codes and quantify the effect of the EC schedules on the correctable operating region below the pseudo-threshold. The 4EC schedule keeps the accuracy of both engines close to one another, making BiBiEQ-Approx a reliable proxy for BiBiEQ-Exact for faster sweeps. Below the pseudo-threshold, the code distance (d) hop from distance (d) 6 to 10 yields a drop in LER by 10-17x larger than distance (d) 10 to 12, showing that most gains are realized by d=10.


---


## 通过量子限制和邻近将非超导体变成超导体

**Original Title:** Turning non-superconducting elements into superconductors by quantum confinement and proximity

**Authors:** Giovanni A. Ummarino, Alessio Zaccone

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07585v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07585v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

元素良金属，包括贵金属（铜、银、金）和几种块元素，在环境压力下不会表现出大块的超导电性，主要是由于弱的电子-音素耦合未能克服库伦排斥。从这个角度来看，我们研究了单独的量子限制或与邻近效应相结合是否会在大块形式的非高温金属中引起可观察到的高温不稳定性。我们回顾了最近的理论进展，并提出了一个基于约束广义、各向同性单带Eliashberg理论的统一框架，其中正常状态密度变得依赖于能量，并且关键材料参数（$E_F$、$A和$μ ' s）获得显着的厚度依赖性。通过使用从头算或实验确定的电子-音素谱函数$a ' a ' F（Q）$和库伦伪势$μ ' u ' s，并且在不引入可调参数的情况下，我们计算了代表性贵金属、碱性金属和碱性金属的临界温度$T_c$作为膜厚度的函数。该理论预测，超导电性只能在选定的情况下和极窄的厚度窗口内出现，通常以亚纳米尺度为中心（$L \sim 0.4$--$0.6$~纳米）。我们进一步讨论了量子限制和邻近效应共存的分层超导体/普通金属系统。在这些异相结构中，预测临界温度会大幅提高，即使组成材料是非超导体或大块形式的不良超导体。


### Abstract

Elemental good metals, including noble metals (Cu, Ag, Au) and several $s$-block elements, do not exhibit superconductivity in bulk at ambient pressure, primarily due to weak electron--phonon coupling that fails to overcome Coulomb repulsion. In this perspective, we examine whether quantum confinement alone, or in combination with proximity effects, can induce an observable superconducting instability in metals that are non-superconducting in bulk form. We review recent theoretical progress and present a unified framework based on a confinement-generalized, isotropic one-band Eliashberg theory, in which the normal density of states becomes energy dependent and key material parameters ($E_F$, $λ$, and $μ^{*}$) acquire an explicit thickness dependence. By numerically solving the resulting Eliashberg equations using ab-initio or experimentally determined electron--phonon spectral functions $α^{2}F(Ω)$ and Coulomb pseudopotentials $μ^{*}$, and without introducing adjustable parameters, we compute the critical temperature $T_c$ as a function of film thickness for representative noble, alkali, and alkaline-earth metals. The theory predicts that superconductivity can emerge only in selected cases and within extremely narrow thickness windows, typically centered around sub-nanometer scales ($L \sim 0.4$--$0.6$~nm). We further discuss layered superconductor/normal-metal systems, where quantum confinement and proximity effects coexist. In these heterostructures, a substantial enhancement of the critical temperature is predicted, even when the constituent materials are non-superconducting or poor superconductors in bulk form.

## 量子软件工程导论课程：经验报告

**Original Title:** A Course on the Introduction to Quantum Software Engineering: Experience Report

**Authors:** Andriy Miranskyy

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07589v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07589v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

量子计算越来越多地通过编程实践，但大多数教育课程强调算法或框架级的使用，而不是软件工程问题，例如测试、抽象、工具和生命周期管理。   本文报道了交叉列出的本科-研究生课程的设计和首次提供，该课程通过软件工程角度构建量子计算，重点关注与软件工程实践相关的早期能力。该课程将基础量子概念与软件工程观点相结合，强调可执行工件、经验推理以及概率行为、噪音和不断发展的工具链引起的权衡。证据来自教师观察、学生反馈、调查和学生作业分析。   尽管之前接触过量子计算的机会很少，但一旦建立了对量子信息和量子算法（通过可执行工件表达）的基础理解，学生们就能够富有成效地参与量子软件工程主题。该经验报告为开发量子计算课程的软件工程教育工作者提供了模块化课程设计、针对混合学术水平的可扩展评估模型以及可转移的课程。


### Abstract

Quantum computing is increasingly practiced through programming, yet most educational offerings emphasize algorithmic or framework-level use rather than software engineering concerns such as testing, abstraction, tooling, and lifecycle management.
  This paper reports on the design and first offering of a cross-listed undergraduate--graduate course that frames quantum computing through a software engineering lens, focusing on early-stage competence relevant to software engineering practice. The course integrates foundational quantum concepts with software engineering perspectives, emphasizing executable artifacts, empirical reasoning, and trade-offs arising from probabilistic behaviour, noise, and evolving toolchains. Evidence is drawn from instructor observations, student feedback, surveys, and analysis of student work.
  Despite minimal prior exposure to quantum computing, students were able to engage productively with quantum software engineering topics once a foundational understanding of quantum information and quantum algorithms, expressed through executable artifacts, was established. This experience report contributes a modular course design, a scalable assessment model for mixed academic levels, and transferable lessons for software engineering educators developing quantum computing curricula.

## 关系形式主义背景下的引力诱导的量子退散模型

**Original Title:** A gravitationally induced decoherence model for photons in the context of the relational formalism

**Authors:** Max Joseph Fahn, Kristina Giesel, Roman Kemper

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07622v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07622v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

我们从麦克斯韦理论出发，与线性化引力相结合，制定了一个引力诱导的量子退散模型，用阿什特卡-巴贝罗变量表示，并被视为开放量子场论系统。与量子力学模型相反，系统（麦克斯韦场）和环境（引力场）之间的相互作用并不是现象学上假设的，而是由后明斯克逼近中的潜在作用决定的。该框架扩展了先前的纯量场模型，并能够更详细地分析动态参考场（时钟）在关系形式主义中的作用。我们表明，对于合适地选择几何时钟和U（1）-高斯时钟，并通过采用可观测地图及其二元映射的适当组合，所得的狄拉克可观测量直接由量子场的横向分量以及引力波在耦合系统线性化相空间上的弹性-横向-无痕迹自由度给出。此外，我们还比较了狄拉克可观测量的不同选择及其动态。在对简化系统应用Fock量子化后，我们推导出二阶截断的无时间卷积（TLC）主方程，并分析其结构性质。这些结果为进一步研究退相干模型（包括其重正化和对其单粒子扇形的详细研究）提供了基础，并且发现在结构上与以前使用阿霉素变量和特定规范固定推导出的量子主方程一致。


### Abstract

We formulate a model of gravitationally induced decoherence for photons starting from Maxwell theory coupled to linearised gravity, expressed in terms of Ashtekar-Barbero variables and treated as an open quantum field theoretic system. In contrast to quantum mechanical models, the interaction between the system (Maxwell field) and the environment (gravitational field) is not postulated phenomenologically, but is instead dictated by the underlying action in a post-Minkowskian approximation. This framework extends earlier models for a scalar field and enables a more detailed analysis of the role of dynamical reference fields (clocks) within the relational formalism. We show that, for a suitable choice of geometrical clocks together with a U(1)-Gauss clock, and by employing an appropriate combination of the observable map and its dual, the resulting Dirac observables are given directly by the transverse components of the photon field as well as the symmetric-transverse-traceless degrees of freedom of gravitational waves on the linearised phase space of the coupled system. In addition we also compare different choices of Dirac observables and their dynamics. Upon applying a Fock quantisation to the reduced system, we derive the time convolutionless (TCL) master equation, truncated at second order, and analyse its structural properties. These results provide a foundation for further investigations of the decoherence model, including its renormalisation and a detailed study of its one-particle sector, and are found to be structurally consistent with former master equations for photons derived using ADM variables and a specific gauge fixing.


---


## 磁共振中的隐藏运动学和双量子参考

**Original Title:** Hidden Kinematics and Dual Quantum References in Magnetic Resonance

**Authors:** Sunghyun Kim

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07636v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07636v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

传统上，使用在旋转框架中公式化的转移概率来描述旋转共振现象，其物理意义隐含地取决于量子参考标准的选择。在这次学术讨论会中，我们表明旋转磁场中的旋转构成了涉及两个量子描述的配置，这两个量子描述共享共同的量子化操作符，但其运动学和动力学作用不同。因此，转移概率作为量子参考标准之间的关系量出现，而不是单个演变的旋转状态的固有属性。通过将旋转载体的运动学运动与动力学演变结合起来，该框架恢复了一致的能量核算，并揭示了旋转磁场中旋转动力学背后的双参考结构。


### Abstract

Spin resonance phenomena are conventionally described using transition probabilities formulated in a rotating frame, whose physical meaning implicitly depends on the choice of quantum reference standard. In this Colloquium, we show that a spin in a rotating magnetic field constitutes a configuration involving two quantum descriptions that share a common quantization operator but differ in their kinematic and dynamical roles. The transition probability therefore emerges as a relational quantity between quantum reference standards rather than an intrinsic property of a single evolving spin state. By incorporating the kinematic motion of the spin vector together with the dynamical evolution, this framework restores consistent energy accounting and reveals the dual-reference structure underlying spin dynamics in rotating magnetic fields.


---


## 线性射频离子陷阱的两相驱动

**Original Title:** Two-phase driving of a linear radio-frequency ion trap

**Authors:** Santhosh Surendra, Akos Hoffmann, Michael Köhl

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07700v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07700v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-07


### 摘要

线性射频Paul陷阱传统上是通过一对对角电极接地而另一对连接到高压射频源来驱动的。这种方法简化了电压源与陷波器的阻抗匹配。然而，对于几种架构来说，它会导致轴向微运动幅度增加，例如，当射频和端盖电极之间的电容不可忽略时。在这里，我们提出了一种产生两个异相高压射频信号\SI{180}{\degree}的技术，以驱动相邻电极之间电压相反的线性Paul陷阱。利用此，我们成功地在线性射频保罗陷阱中捕获并冷却了一串稀土离子。


### Abstract

A linear radio-frequency Paul trap is traditionally driven with one diagonal pair of electrodes grounded and the other connected to a high-voltage radio-frequency source. This method simplifies impedance matching of the voltage source to the trap. However, for several architectures it leads to increasing the axial micromotion amplitude, for example, when the capacitance between radio-frequency and end-cap electrodes is not negligible. Here, we present a technique to generate two high-voltage radio-frequency signals \SI{180}{\degree} out of phase to drive a linear Paul trap with opposite voltages between neighbouring electrodes. Using this, we have successfully trapped and cooled a chain of Ytterbium ions in a linear radio-frequency Paul trap.


---


## 量子操纵和三体的纠缠：损失下的等级制度

**Original Title:** Quantum Steering and Entanglement in a Tritter: Hierarchy under Loss

**Authors:** Jifeng Sun, Shumin Yang, Teng Zhao, Qingqian Kang, Liyun Hu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07788v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07788v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

连续变量的多方纠缠态是可扩展量子信息处理的基本资源。我们研究了三重状态中的相关层次结构，该三重状态是通过将两模压缩真空与三重状态混合而设计的，三重状态是产生多模式状态的关键线性光学元件。使用协方差矩阵形式主义，我们全面分析了输出模式之间的纠缠和爱因斯坦-波多尔斯基-罗森（Einstein-Podolsky-Rosen）操纵。这两种相关性的强度仅由压缩参数决定，并且与相关幅度无关。我们进一步研究了各种通道配置中不可避免的光损失的影响。结果表明，虽然损失会降低相关性，但EPR转向仍然是一夫一妻制，并且表现出比纠缠更严格的弹性阈值。我们的分析在参数扩展技术的支持下证实了引导条件比不可分离性标准更严格，清楚地表明引导形成了纠缠的严格子集。这些结果阐明了容易生成的多模式状态中的相关结构，并为开发不对称量子协议（例如单边设备独立任务）提供了实用见解，其中EPR引导是关键资源。


### Abstract

Multipartite entangled states of continuous variables are fundamental resources for scalable quantum information processing. We study the correlation hierarchy in a tripartite state engineered by mixing a two-mode squeezed vacuum with a coherent state on a tritter, a key linear optical element for multimode state generation. Using the covariance matrix formalism, we comprehensively analyze the entanglement and Einstein-Podolsky-Rosen (EPR) steering among the output modes. The strength of both correlations is governed solely by the squeezing parameter and is independent of the coherent amplitude. We further examine the impact of inevitable optical losses in various channel configurations. The results show that while losses degrade correlations, EPR steering remains monogamous and exhibits stricter resilience thresholds than entanglement. Our analysis, supported by parameter extension techniques, confirms that the steering condition is more stringent than the inseparability criterion, clearly demonstrating that steering forms a strict subset of entanglement. These results elucidate the correlation structure in a readily generated multimode state and offer practical insights for developing asymmetric quantum protocols, such as one-sided device-independent tasks, where EPR steering serves as a critical resource.

## 驱动Jaynes-Cummings模型中的几何临界性

**Original Title:** Geometric criticality in the driven Jaynes-Cummings model

**Authors:** Ken Chen, Jia-Hao Lv, Hao-Long Zhang, Fan Wu, Wen Ning, Zhen-Biao Yang, Shi-Biao Zheng

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07795v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07795v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

当Jaynes-Cummings模型中的光模受外部经典场驱动时，系统会在临界点发生光阻挡击穿相转变。这种相转变已经得到了详细的研究，但到目前为止，本征态的临界性质在很大程度上仍未被探索。我们在这里研究与这些本征状态相关的几何临界性。驱动器的幅度和相作为统治Hamilton的控制参数。我们发现每个本征态的量子度规和贝瑞弯曲张量在临界区域表现出不同的行为。更重要的是，与亮本征态相关的分歧比独特暗态的分歧要明显得多。我们的理论结果可以在电路量子电动力学系统中得到实验证实，其中驱动Jaynes-Cummings模型已经实现。


### Abstract

When the photonic mode in the Jaynes-Cummings model is driven by an external classical field, the system can undergo the photon-blockade breakdown phase transition at a critical point. Such a phase transition has been detailedly investigated, but the critical properties of the eigenstates remain largely unexplored so far. We here study the geometric criticality associated with these eigenstates. The amplitude and phase of the drive serve as the control parameter of the governing Hamiltonian. We find the quantum metric and Berry curvature tensors for each eigenstate display divergent behaviors in the critical region. More importantly, the divergence associated with bright eigenstates is much more pronounced than that for the unique dark state. Our theoretical results can be experimentally confirmed in circuit quantum electrodynamics systems, where the driven Jaynes-Cummings model has been realized.


---


## 多维量子通道的半设备独立认证

**Original Title:** Semi-device-independent certification of high-dimensional quantum channels

**Authors:** Mengyan Li, Yanning Jia, Fenzhuo Guo, Haifeng Dong, Sujuan Qin, Fei Gao

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07823v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07823v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

验证高维量子信道对于确保量子通信协议的可靠性至关重要。现有的认证方案通常依赖于完全可信的内部设备，这在现实场景中很难实现。在这里，我们提出了一个半设备独立的框架，直接从观察到的统计数据，假设只有系统的尺寸是已知的认证信道属性。通过明确地将完整的结构约束固有的Choi状态，我们的方法利用Choi-Jamiovakowski同构严格认证的量子通道。量子通道的纠缠维度首先通过引入见证并在数字上确定其与施密特数相关的边界来证明。该认证方法复制了已知的分析基准，并应用于去相和去极化噪音通道，从而确认其有效性。为了提供更完整的通道性能评估，量子通道的纠缠保真度还使用基于局部化矩阵的半定编程松弛层次结构来认证。获得了纠缠保真度的下限，该下限与完整的观察统计数据或单个见证值兼容。


### Abstract

Certifying high-dimensional quantum channels is essential for ensuring the reliability of quantum communication protocols. Existing certification schemes often rely on fully trusted internal devices, which is difficult to achieve in realistic scenarios. Here, we propose a semi-device-independent framework for certifying channel properties directly from observed statistics, assuming only that the system dimension is known. By explicitly incorporating the full set of structural constraints inherent to Choi states, our approach exploits the Choi-Jamiołkowski isomorphism for rigorous certification of quantum channels. The entanglement dimensionality of quantum channels is first certified by introducing a witness and numerically determining its Schmidt-number-dependent bounds. This certification method reproduces known analytical benchmarks and is applied to dephasing and depolarizing noise channels, thereby confirming its validity. To provide a more complete assessment of channel performance, the entanglement fidelity of quantum channels is also certified using a hierarchy of semidefinite programming relaxations based on localizing matrices. Lower bounds on the entanglement fidelity are obtained that are compatible with either the full set of observed statistics or a single witness value.

## 结构近轴电子的几何使能辐射

**Original Title:** Geometry-Enabled Radiation from Structured Paraxial Electrons

**Authors:** M. S. Epov, I. E. Shenderovich, S. S. Baturin

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07858v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07858v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

我们对扭曲（近轴）电子在非均匀、轴对称磁场中传播的自发量子发射进行了微观计算。我们通过将Foldy-Wouthuysen变换与基于Lewis-Ermakov不变量和元辛变换的几何框架相结合，构建了包含横模结构和波阵面弯曲的精确电子状态。我们表明，这种结构化状态的演变对应于二次型空间中的开放路径，从而对发射幅度产生几何贡献，而这种贡献无法通过规范选择或隔热参数来消除。电子波阵面的反弯曲半径作为有效的几何场出现，即使在外部磁场局部消失的区域也能产生辐射。这种机制将兰道级辐射推广到非渐进的结构化电子状态，并在非循环几何进化和量子发射之间建立了直接联系。


### Abstract

We present a microscopic calculation of spontaneous photon emission by twisted (paraxial) electrons propagating through inhomogeneous, axisymmetric magnetic fields. We construct exact electron states that incorporate transverse mode structure and wavefront curvature by combining the Foldy-Wouthuysen transformation with a geometric framework based on Lewis-Ermakov invariants and metaplectic transformations. We show that the evolution of such structured states corresponds to an open path in the space of quadratic forms, giving rise to a geometric contribution to the emission amplitude that cannot be eliminated by gauge choice or adiabatic arguments. The inverse radius of curvature of the electron wavefront emerges as an effective geometric field that enables radiation even in regions where the external magnetic field vanishes locally. This mechanism generalizes Landau-level radiation to nonasymptotic, structured electron states and establishes a direct connection between noncyclic geometric evolution and photon emission.

## 具有三位点相互作用的最小不可积模型

**Original Title:** Minimal nonintegrable models with three-site interactions

**Authors:** Wen-Ming Fan, Kun Hao, Xiao-Hui Wang, Kun Zhang, Vladimir Korepin

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07867v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07867v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

仍然缺乏对具有真正三位点相互作用的热力不变旋转链中可积性破坏的系统了解。在这项工作中，我们引入了最小不可积的旋转-$1/2$Hamilton，并对其进行了分类，该模型被定义为使内射性饱和，同时不允许除Hamilton之外的非平凡局部保守电荷。我们首先通过将变形弗雷德金旋转链映射到最近邻复合旋转表示并排除所有可接受的3美元局部保守荷，严格建立了具有周期边界条件的变形弗雷德金旋转链的不可积性。在其结构的指导下，我们构建了五类具有真正三位点相互作用的旋转1/2美元模型。一类是可积的，而其余四类恰好包含两个交互项，并构成最小的不可积的三站点模型。我们的结果在最近邻范式之外描绘了可集成性和不可集成性之间的尖锐界限。


### Abstract

A systematic understanding of integrability breaking in translationally invariant spin chains with genuine three-site interactions remains lacking. In this work, we introduce and classify minimal nonintegrable spin-$1/2$ Hamiltonians, defined as models that saturate injectivity while admitting no nontrivial local conserved charges beyond the Hamiltonian. We first rigorously establish the nonintegrability of the deformed Fredkin spin chain with periodic boundary conditions by mapping it to a nearest-neighbor composite-spin representation and excluding all admissible $3$-local conserved charges. Guided by its structure, we then construct five classes of spin-$1/2$ models with genuine three-site interactions. One class is integrable, while the remaining four contain exactly two interaction terms and constitute the minimal nonintegrable three-site models. Our results delineate a sharp boundary between integrability and nonintegrability beyond the nearest-neighbor paradigm.

## 霍普夫代数Hamilton体的量子进化

**Original Title:** Quantum Evolution of Hopf Algebra Hamiltonians

**Authors:** Michele Arzano, Antonio Del Prete, Domenico Frattulillo

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07887v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07887v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

近年来，越来越多的注意力被投入到这样一种可能性上：与某些非交换时空模型相关的具有变形对称性的理论可能会编码一种基本形式的退相干。这种效应应该用类似Lindblad的进化来描述，该进化由时间进化生成器的非平凡霍普夫代数结构控制。在这项工作中，我们对量子位Hamilton的类似霍普夫代数变形的这种可能性进行了详细分析。我们从通过广义伴随作用对时间演变的定义进行批判性检查开始，探索是否可以建立一个连贯且物理上可行的框架。特别是，我们的分析表明，伴随作用的更一般组合总是保证冯·诺伊曼动力学，而且，在文献中考虑的变形时空对称性的情况下，物理上可行的林德布拉德进化无法建立。


### Abstract

In recent years, growing attention has been devoted to the possibility that theories with deformed symmetries, associated with certain models of non-commutative spacetime, may encode a fundamental form of decoherence. This effect should be described by a Lindblad-like evolution governed by the non-trivial Hopf algebra structure of the time-evolution generators. In this work we provide a detailed analysis of such possibility for similar Hopf algebra deformations of the Hamiltonian of a qubit. Starting from a critical examination of the very definition of time evolution through the generalized adjoint action, we explore whether a coherent and physically viable framework can be established. In particular, our analysis shows that a more general combination of adjoint actions always guarantees a von Neumann dynamics and, also in the case of deformed spacetime symmetries considered in the literature, a physically viable Lindblad evolution cannot be established.

## 探索全息共形场论

**Original Title:** Probing holographic conformal field theories

**Authors:** Ming Zhang, Jiayue Yang, Dyuman Bhattacharya, Robert B. Mann

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07895v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07895v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

我们引入了一个可操作的、边界优先的框架，通过将Unruh-DeWitt检测器直接耦合到全息CFT的局部纯量初级操作符，将相对论量子信息协议嵌入到反德西特/共形场论（AdS/CFT）中。使用通用CFT Wightman函数，我们微扰地计算探测器的约化密度操作符，同时保留激发概率和相干性。作为一个具体的资源理论应用，我们使用qutrit探针实现了魔法资源（魔法力）收获。对于CFT与全局AdS的二元，我们表明所收获的魔法力明显区分了Breitenlohner-Freedman窗口中的两个可接受的纯量量化，标准量化产生的魔法力比替代量化产生的系统性更大。我们的结果提供了一种通过量子信息源测试全息原理的可行方法。


### Abstract

We introduce an operational, boundary-first framework that embeds relativistic quantum-information protocols into anti-de Sitter/Conformal Field Theory (AdS/CFT) by coupling an Unruh--DeWitt detector directly to a local scalar primary operator of a holographic CFT. Using the universal CFT Wightman function, we compute the detector's reduced density operator perturbatively, retaining both excitation probabilities and coherences. As a concrete resource-theoretic application, we implement magic resource (mana) harvesting with a qutrit probe. For a CFT dual to global AdS, we show that the harvested mana sharply distinguishes the two admissible scalar quantizations in the Breitenlohner--Freedman window, with the standard quantization yielding systematically larger mana than the alternate one. Our results provide a viable way of testing holography principle through quantum information resource.


---


## 基于零级空间的量子选择配置相互作用大小加倍及其在QC-QSCI-AFQMC中的应用

**Original Title:** Doubling the size of quantum selected configuration interaction based on seniority-zero space and its application to QC-QSCI-AFQMC

**Authors:** Yuichiro Yoshida, Takuma Murokoshi, Naoya Kuroda, Wataru Mizukami

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07912v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07912v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

我们提出了双占据配置相互作用-量子选择配置相互作用（DOCI-QSCI），它从零级空间进行采样。虽然这个空间的使用实际上使量子位预算增加了一倍，相当于空间轨道的数量，但这种部门限制可能会损害量化准确性。为了弥补这一点，我们通过其Cartesian积将采样的位串扩展到一个更大的空间中，其中包括破坏优先级的决定因素。还提出了使用无相辅助场量子蒙特卡罗（ph-AFQMC）中的试验状态来恢复整个轨道空间的动态相关性（DOCI-QSCI-AFQMC）。我们评估了H6链、N2分解和向BODIPY染料添加单重态O2的方法。对于H6链，DOCI-QSCI-AFQMC用量子设备ibm kobe重现了完全活跃空间对应物的水平准确性。对于N2和BODIPY-O2，具有（14 e，28 o）和最高（20 e，20 o）有效空间，它会产生合理的结果，而单参考CCSD（T）在定性上失败。这些结果表明，DOCI-QSCI将传统QSCI可访问的轨道空间增加了一倍，随后的ph-AFQMC后处理可提供相当高的准确性。


### Abstract

We propose doubly occupied configuration interaction-quantum selected configuration interaction (DOCI-QSCI), which samples from the seniority-zero space. While the use of this space effectively doubles the qubit budget, equaling the number of spatial orbitals, this sector restriction can compromise quantitative accuracy. To compensate for this, we expand sampled bitstrings via their Cartesian product into a larger space that includes seniority-breaking determinants. The resulting wave function is also proposed using the trial state in phaseless auxiliary-field quantum Monte Carlo (ph-AFQMC) to recover dynamical correlations across the full orbital space (DOCI-QSCI-AFQMC). We evaluate the proposed methods on the H6 chain, N2 dissociation, and the addition of singlet O2 to a BODIPY dye. For the H6 chain, DOCI-QSCI-AFQMC reproduces the accuracy of the level of the complete-active-space counterpart with the quantum device ibm kobe. For N2 and BODIPY-O2, with (14e, 28o) and up to (20e, 20o) active spaces, it yields reasonable results, whereas single-reference CCSD(T) fails qualitatively. These results demonstrate that the DOCI-QSCI doubles the orbital space accessible to conventional QSCI and subsequent ph-AFQMC post-processing delivers reasonably high accuracy.


---


## 作为QUBO问题的多智能体路线规划

**Original Title:** Multi-Agent Route Planning as a QUBO Problem

**Authors:** Renáta Rusnáková, Martin Chovanec, Juraj Gazda

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07913v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07913v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

多代理路线规划考虑选择车辆，每辆车辆与一条预定义路线关联，以便增加道路网络的空间覆盖范围，同时限制冗余重叠。本文给出了一个形式化的问题定义，通过从加权集包装问题中约简证明了NP困难性，并推导出二次无约束二元优化公式，其系数直接编码唯一覆盖回报和成对重叠惩罚。单个罚参数控制覆盖率-重叠权衡。我们区分了支持多目标探索的软制度和硬制度，其中惩罚足够强，可以有效执行近乎不相交的路线。我们描述了一个实际的管道，用于生成城市实例、构建候选路线、构建QUBO矩阵，并使用精确混合整解算器（Guidelines）、模拟模拟在拥有多达10，000辆车的巴塞罗那实例上进行的实验揭示了明显的覆盖重叠膝盖，并表明帕累托最优解主要是在硬罚制度下获得的，而D-Wave混合解算器和Guidelty实现了基本相同的目标值，随着问题规模的增长，运行时间只有微小差异。


### Abstract

Multi-Agent Route Planning considers selecting vehicles, each associated with a single predefined route, such that the spatial coverage of a road network is increased while redundant overlaps are limited. This paper gives a formal problem definition, proves NP-hardness by reduction from the Weighted Set Packing problem, and derives a Quadratic Unconstrained Binary Optimization formulation whose coefficients directly encode unique coverage rewards and pairwise overlap penalties. A single penalty parameter controls the coverage-overlap trade-off. We distinguish between a soft regime, which supports multi-objective exploration, and a hard regime, in which the penalty is strong enough to effectively enforce near-disjoint routes. We describe a practical pipeline for generating city instances, constructing candidate routes, building the QUBO matrix, and solving it with an exact mixed-integer solver (Gurobi), simulated annealing, and D-Wave hybrid quantum annealing. Experiments on Barcelona instances with up to 10 000 vehicles reveal a clear coverage-overlap knee and show that Pareto-optimal solutions are mainly obtained under the hard-penalty regime, while D-Wave hybrid solvers and Gurobi achieve essentially identical objective values with only minor differences in runtime as problem size grows.


---


## 基于微波频率调制光电流的金刚石氮空位中心实时磁场传感

**Original Title:** Real-Time Magnetic Field Sensing based on Microwave Frequency Modulated Photocurrent of Nitrogen-Vacancy Centers in Diamond

**Authors:** Xuan-Ming Shen, Qilong Wu, Huihui Yu, Pei-Nan Ni, Qing Lou, Chao-Nan Lin, Xun Yang, Chong-Xin Shan, Yuan Zhang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07926v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07926v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

虽然磁共振光电检测（PDMR）可用于微型化基于氮空位（NV）中心的量子传感器，但基于PDMR的磁场传感的真实演示仍然是一个独特的挑战。为了应对这一挑战，本文中我们制作了表面带有电极和微波天线的金刚石样品，并通过各种锁定放大模式检测纳安范围内的光电流来实现PDMR。重要的是，我们获得了激光强度和微波频率调制模式在DC-10 Hz范围内磁场检测的理论和实验灵敏度分别为397 nT/Hz和921 nT/Hz，并首次展示了对交流磁场的实时跟踪，标准差为1.5 uT。此外，我们系统地研究了PDMR对比度、谱线宽度和灵敏度对激光和微波功率的依赖性，并发现与基于主方程的理论模型完全一致，该模型不仅考虑了中性和负NV中心的光致电荷开关，还考虑了与微波场的相互作用。


### Abstract

While photoelectric detection of magnetic resonance (PDMR) can be applied to miniaturize nitrogen-vacancy (NV) center-based quantum sensors, the real demonstration of PDMR-based magnetic field sensing remains as a distinctive challenge. To tackle this challenge, in this article, we fabricate diamond samples with electrodes and microwave antenna on the surface, and realize PDMR by detecting photocurrent in nanoampere range via various lock-in amplifying modes. Importantly, we obtain a theoretical and experimental sensitivity 397 nT/Hz and 921 nT/Hz of magnetic field detection in DC-10 Hz range with a laser intensity and microwave frequency modulated mode, respectively, and demonstrate for the first time, a real-time tracking of alternating magnetic field with a standard deviation of 1.5 uT. Furthermore, we investigate systematically the dependence of the PDMR contrast, linewidth and the sensitivity on the laser and microwave power, and find a perfect agreement with a master equation based theoretical model, which accounts for not only the optically induced charge switch of neutral and negative NV centers, but also the interaction with microwave field.

## 一种基于量子启发的非线性偏出方程的多层张量列单片时空方法

**Original Title:** A quantum-inspired multi-level tensor-train monolithic space-time method for nonlinear PDEs

**Authors:** N. R. Rapaka, R. Peddinti, E. Tiunov, N. J. Faraj, A. N. Alkhooori, L. Aolita, Y. Addad, M. K. Riahi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07945v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07945v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

本文提出了一个求解全局时空非线性偏微分方程的多级张量序列框架。虽然时空TT求解器已经证明了压缩高维模拟的巨大潜力，但文献中几乎没有与经典时间步进方法进行系统比较，有限的误差收敛分析，以及TT舍入对数值精度的影响的定量评估。同样，现有的研究未能证明在不同PDE和参数范围内的性能。在实践中，单片牛顿迭代可能会停滞或无法收敛在强非线性，僵硬，或对流主导的制度，其中穷人的初始猜测和严重病态的时空雅可比矩阵阻碍鲁棒收敛。我们通过引入完全嵌入TT格式中的从粗到细的多层策略来克服这一限制。每个级别都细化了空间和时间分辨率，同时通过低阶延拓运算符传输TT解，为连续的牛顿解提供稳健的初始化。剩余量、雅可比量和转移运算符直接在TT中表示，并使用自适应排序DMRG算法求解。对包括Fisher-KPP、粘性Burgers、sine-Gordon和Kdis在内的一系列非线性偏出方程的数值实验涵盖了扩散、对流和频散动力学，证明了多层TT方法在单级时空牛顿迭代失败的地方始终收敛。在动态的、以平流为主的（非线性）场景中，多层TT优于单级TT，在显着降低计算成本的情况下实现高准确度，特别是在需要高保真度数值模拟时。


### Abstract

We propose a multilevel tensor-train (TT) framework for solving nonlinear partial differential equations (PDEs) in a global space-time formulation. While space-time TT solvers have demonstrated significant potential for compressed high-dimensional simulations, the literature contains few systematic comparisons with classical time-stepping methods, limited error convergence analyses, and little quantitative assessment of the impact of TT rounding on numerical accuracy. Likewise, existing studies fail to demonstrate performance across a diverse set of PDEs and parameter ranges. In practice, monolithic Newton iterations may stagnate or fail to converge in strongly nonlinear, stiff, or advection-dominated regimes, where poor initial guesses and severely ill-conditioned space-time Jacobians hinder robust convergence. We overcome this limitation by introducing a coarse-to-fine multilevel strategy fully embedded within the TT format. Each level refines both spatial and temporal resolutions while transferring the TT solution through low-rank prolongation operators, providing robust initializations for successive Newton solves. Residuals, Jacobians, and transfer operators are represented directly in TT and solved with the adaptive-rank DMRG algorithm. Numerical experiments for a selection of nonlinear PDEs including Fisher-KPP, viscous Burgers, sine-Gordon, and KdV cover diffusive, convective, and dispersive dynamics, demonstrating that the multilevel TT approach consistently converges where single-level space-time Newton iterations fail. In dynamic, advection-dominated (nonlinear) scenarios, multilevel TT surpasses single-level TT, achieving high accuracy with significantly reduced computational cost, specifically when high-fidelity numerical simulation is required.


---


## 自发参量下转换产生的时空纠缠态的Schmidt全刻划

**Original Title:** Full Schmidt characterization of spatiotemporally entangled states produced from spontaneous parametric down-conversion

**Authors:** Rakesh Pradhan, Girish Kulkarni

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07949v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07949v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

由于自发参数下转换（SPDC）产生的时空纠缠态的大维度计算复杂性，迄今为止尚未对自发参数下转换（SPDC）产生的时空纠缠态进行完整施密特分解。在这封信中，我们利用状态的旋转对称性将复杂性降低至少四个数量级，并进行分解以揭示时空施密特模和跨越104个模的施密特谱的精确形式。我们表明，施密特模的相轮廓具有横向空间涡旋结构，这赋予它们在所有频率下的轨道角动量。在高收益区，随着抽运强度的增加，这些施密特模式变宽，施密特光谱变窄。我们的工作可以在利用SPDC产生的纠缠态的量子成像和光谱学交叉点激发新的应用。


### Abstract

The full Schmidt decomposition of spatiotemporally entangled states generated from spontaneous parametric down-conversion (SPDC) has not been carried out until now due to the immense computational complexity arising from the large dimensionalities of the states. In this Letter, we utilize the rotational symmetry of the states to reduce the complexity by at least four orders of magnitude and carry out the decomposition to reveal the precise forms of the spatiotemporal Schmidt modes and the Schmidt spectrum spanning over 10^4 modes. We show that the Schmidt modes have a phase profile with a transverse spatial vortex structure that endows them with orbital angular momentum at all frequencies. In the high-gain regime, these Schmidt modes broaden and the Schmidt spectrum narrows with increasing pump strength. Our work can spur novel applications at the intersection of quantum imaging and spectroscopy that utilize entangled states produced from SPDC.


---


## 布朗旋转SYK模型中扰频动力学的高级修正

**Original Title:** Higher-Order Corrections to Scrambling Dynamics in Brownian Spin SYK Models

**Authors:** Tingfei Li, Miao Wang, Jianghui Yu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07952v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07952v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

我们研究了具有随机全对全相互作用的布朗旋转Sachdev--Ye--Kitaev（SYK）模型中的操作符增长，重点关注完整的操作符大小分布。对于包含二阶至$L$的相互作用的Hamilton方程，我们推导出Pauli弦展开系数的封闭主方程，并将其动力学重新转换为适合大$N$极限的生成函数公式。这种方法使我们能够显式地对角化领先阶进化操作符，并获得任意初始操作符分布的精确解，包括去相关的影响。超越领先订单，我们开发了系统性的1美元/N美元扩张，捕捉对运营商规模动态和后期行为的更高层修正。我们的结果表明，更高级效应在操作符扰乱中发挥着至关重要的作用，并且完整的操作符大小分布为布朗和开放量子系统中的量子混乱提供了更精确的探测。


### Abstract

We investigate operator growth in a Brownian spin Sachdev--Ye--Kitaev (SYK) model with random all-to-all interactions, focusing on the full operator-size distribution. For Hamiltonians containing interactions of order two up to $L$, we derive a closed master equation for the Pauli-string expansion coefficients and recast their dynamics into a generating-function formulation suitable for the large-$N$ limit. This approach allows us to diagonalize the leading-order evolution operator explicitly and obtain exact solutions for arbitrary initial operator distributions, including the effects of decoherence. Going beyond leading order, we develop a systematic $1/N$ expansion that captures higher-order corrections to the operator-size dynamics and the late-time behavior. Our results demonstrate that higher-order effects play a crucial role in operator scrambling and that the full operator-size distribution provides a more refined probe of quantum chaos in Brownian and open quantum systems.


---


## 无限深空腔内的量子自相互作用

**Original Title:** Quantum self-interaction within an infinitely deep cavity

**Authors:** Sergio Giardino

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07956v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07956v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

我们可以在真正的希尔伯特空间的框架内考察无限深量子腔，也称为量子无限方井。根据复波函数以及四元数波函数来考虑解。复杂的结果重现了在复杂的希尔伯特空间中建立的通常成果，但也将它们扩展到非稳态解，以及扭曲的稳态解、不同的能谱和错位的观察位置。四元数案例进一步承认了自我相互作用的发生，这是在复杂的解决方案中无法观察到的。因此，复解和四元数解都比以前的情况更一般，从而为在非相对论理论中进一步研究一维解开辟了道路。


### Abstract

One examines the infinitely deep quantum cavity, also known as the quantum infinite square well, within the framework of the real Hilbert space. The solutions are considered in terms of complex wave functions, and also in terms of quaternionic wave functions. The complex results reproduce the usual achievements established in the complex Hilbert space, but also extend them to non-stationary solutions, as well as to distorted stationary solutions, different energy spectra, and dislocated observed position. The quaternionic cases further admit the incidence of self-interaction, something that cannot be observed in complex solutions. Therefore, both the complex and quaternionic solutions are more general than previous cases, thus opening the way to further one-dimensional solutions to be researched in the non-relativistic theory.


---


## 利用线性光学改进的基于纠缠的多维光学量子计算

**Original Title:** Improved entanglement-based high-dimensional optical quantum computation with linear optics

**Authors:** Huan-Chao Gao, Guo-Zhu Song, Hai-Rui Wei

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2602.07971v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2602.07971v1

**Submitted:** 2026-02-08


### 摘要

量子门是量子计算机的重要模块。对于某些量子信息处理任务，一维量子门比二维量子门表现出显着的优势。在这里，我们在$\mathbb{C}^{2}上展示了一系列基于纠缠的光学受控SWAP门。\otimes\mathbb {C}^{d}$。通过混合编码，我们分别以光极化和空间自由度对控制量子比特和目标量子比特进行编码。该电路仅使用$（2+3d）$（$d\geq 2$）线性光学器件构建，击败了14个线性光学器件的早期结果，$d=2$。电路深度5远低于早期结果11（$d=2$）。此外，该电路的保真度可达99.4%，高于之前的$d=2$的电路。我们的方案是以确定性的方式构建的，没有任何借来的辅助量子或测量引起的非线性。此外，我们的方法允许$d>2$。


### Abstract

Quantum gates are the essential block for quantum computer. High-dimensional quantum gates exhibit remarkable advantages over their two-dimensional counterparts for some quantum information processing tasks. Here we present a family of entanglement-based optical controlled-SWAP gates on $\mathbb{C}^{2}\otimes \mathbb{C}^{d}\otimes \mathbb{C}^{d}$. With the hybrid encoding, we encode the control qubits and target qudits in photonic polarization and spatial degrees of freedom, respectively. The circuit is constructed using only $(2+3d)$ ($d\geq 2$) linear optics, beating an earlier result of 14 linear optics with $d=2$. The circuit depth 5 is much lower than an earlier result of 11 with $d=2$. Besides, the fidelity of the presented circuit can reach 99.4\%, and it is higher than the previous counterpart with $d=2$. Our scheme are constructed in a deterministic way without any borrowed ancillary photons or measurement-induced nonlinearities. Moreover, our approach allows $d>2$.
